function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

}

if (is_file('dev/logo/logo.png') && (sha1_file('dev/logo/logo.png') != '18ddcece6df95ebfebdf43adcba6cee6d070d9a2')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/logo/logo.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('dev/logo/logo.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/logo/logo.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('dev/logo/logo.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('dev/logo/logo.png')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/logo/logo.png');
} else if (sha1_file('dev/logo/logo.png') != '18ddcece6df95ebfebdf43adcba6cee6d070d9a2') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/logo/logo.png');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/logo/logo.png', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/logo/logo.png');
}

if (is_file('dev/logo/logo_anim.gif') && (sha1_file('dev/logo/logo_anim.gif') != '4f0e357e9423dfb58b1e8e8dd06da13acdbe4eca')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/logo/logo_anim.gif');
	$tmp = pathinfo('dev/logo/logo_anim.gif');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/logo/logo_anim.gif')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('dev/logo/logo_anim.gif', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_2();
if (!is_file('dev/logo/logo_anim.gif')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/logo/logo_anim.gif');
} else if (sha1_file('dev/logo/logo_anim.gif') != '4f0e357e9423dfb58b1e8e8dd06da13acdbe4eca') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/logo/logo_anim.gif');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/logo/logo_anim.gif', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/logo/logo_anim.gif');
}

if (is_file('dev/logo/logo_anim.psd') && (sha1_file('dev/logo/logo_anim.psd') != '13953518d78c621942f3aaed4400b91703b750cc')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/logo/logo_anim.psd');
	$tmp = pathinfo('dev/logo/logo_anim.psd');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/logo/logo_anim.psd')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('dev/logo/logo_anim.psd', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_3();
if (!is_file('dev/logo/logo_anim.psd')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/logo/logo_anim.psd');
} else if (sha1_file('dev/logo/logo_anim.psd') != '13953518d78c621942f3aaed4400b91703b750cc') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/logo/logo_anim.psd');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/logo/logo_anim.psd', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/logo/logo_anim.psd');
}

if (is_file('plugins/design/default/logo_anim.gif') && (sha1_file('plugins/design/default/logo_anim.gif') != '4f0e357e9423dfb58b1e8e8dd06da13acdbe4eca')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/design/default/logo_anim.gif');
	$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/design/default/logo_anim.gif');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/design/default/logo_anim.gif')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('plugins/design/default/logo_anim.gif', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_4();
if (!is_file('plugins/design/default/logo_anim.gif')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/design/default/logo_anim.gif');
} else if (sha1_file('plugins/design/default/logo_anim.gif') != '4f0e357e9423dfb58b1e8e8dd06da13acdbe4eca') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/design/default/logo_anim.gif');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/design/default/logo_anim.gif', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/design/default/logo_anim.gif');
}

	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/design/ironbase/logo_anim.gif');
	$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/design/ironbase/logo_anim.gif');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/design/ironbase/logo_anim.gif')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('plugins/design/ironbase/logo_anim.gif', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}

	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/design/ironbase/logo_anim.gif');

	warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/design/ironbase/logo_anim.gif');
}

	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css') != '65b381eaaf6e334943b11d4d1e97e4d0fbc7472b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css') !== '65b381eaaf6e334943b11d4d1e97e4d0fbc7472b') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css') !== '1444d46e8aa68d691b6e3c4f22e49e50a9bbc989') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css') !== '65b381eaaf6e334943b11d4d1e97e4d0fbc7472b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
		}
	}

if (!is_file('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css') != 'cba0ae6de4c6cdec8f986228d6b55fe17f46d9ec') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css') !== 'cba0ae6de4c6cdec8f986228d6b55fe17f46d9ec') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css') !== '3b2520550c7d45ab36ce853fd04af99711153b3e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css') !== 'cba0ae6de4c6cdec8f986228d6b55fe17f46d9ec') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
		}
	}
}
